Today's speed work lasted 70 minutes which equaled about 8.15 total miles. Everyday I'm slowly but surely building mileage and working to beat yesterday. For me the hardest part of marathon training is not completing the workouts, but trusting the plan . 
During my cool down I spotted this arrow. It's purpose was to direct wakers, but for me it served as a reminder that we have the ability to choose the paths we take. Don't make your choices out of fear. Rather, make them with a goal of purpose and fulfillment in mind and soul. This means something different for everyone! It is not always the path of least resistance and often times it is hard to see the finish line. Don't forget that it is never too late to go your own way, blaze a trail, and make a path. You've just got to trust it and find your Happy. Today's speed work lasted 70 minutes which equaled about 8.15 total miles. Everyday I'm slowly but surely building mileage and working to beat yesterday. For me the hardest part of marathon training is not completing the workouts, but trusting the plan . 
During my cool down I spotted this arrow. It's purpose was to direct wakers, but for me it served as a reminder that we have the ability to choose the paths we take. Don't make your choices out of fear. Rather, make them with a goal of purpose and fulfillment in mind and soul. This means something different for everyone! It is not always the path of least resistance and often times it is hard to see the finish line. Don't forget that it is never too late to go your own way, blaze a trail, and make a path. You've just got to trust it and find your Happy. Today's speed work lasted 70 minutes which equaled about 8.15 total miles. Everyday I'm slowly but surely building mileage and working to beat yesterday. For me the hardest part of marathon training is not completing the workouts, but trusting the plan . 
During my cool down I spotted this arrow. It's purpose was to direct wakers, but for me it served as a reminder that we have the ability to choose the paths we take.
